pa dyaloge syr thomas knyghte one counsayll oure souerayne lorde kyng chauncellour hys duchy lancaster wherin treatyd dyuers mater veneration worshyp ymagys relyques prayng sayntys goyng pylgrymage wyth many othere thyngys touchyng pestylent sect luther tyndale tone bygone saxony tother laboryd brought englond preface phyt y olde sayd saw one bysynes bygettyth bryngeth forthe nother whych prouerbe hit happeth fynde trew selfe whych haue bene fayne occasyo first one busygnes er take second vppo seconde take thyrd ryght worshyp ull fred myne sent ny vnto secret sure frende hys wyth certayne credence declared vnto towchyng many mater beyng dede certayne owte doute nethelesse late lewd peple put questy specyaltees whereof doo ferforth furst chapyter thys boke appere shall nede rehersall therof thought yt fyrst inough tell ye messeger mynd mouth accoptyng yt af er comunycacyon ended shuld neuer nede ferther busynes therin messenger departed felte stomake well eased yt rekened laboure done thynkyng selfe lytle whyle theron busynes toke fynyshed fo nd farre fro poynt lytle bygonne whan consydred matter many greate thingys bene treated bytwene messenger maner fashyone albe mystrustyd good wyll well trustede hys wyt lernyng well seruyng hym perseuyng reportyng comunycacyon yet fyndyng oure treatye dyuerse long sumetyme wyse intrycate self could wythout labour call orderly mind thought well done wythout wrytynge trust hys onely memory namely sith sum part mater theym selfe rather nede attentely redde aduysed tha houerly hard passyd ouer ouer cosidred yt thogh nothynge suspecte messenger good faythe saye ye trouthe self lytle mystrustyng ke pl ynly shew hym selfe nought shulde take badde yet sith man ca loke nothers breste yt y therfore well done deme beste yt mich amysse sych wyse uyde worste yf man happe worse tha take good opynyon turne v none harme thys cause thought ye suertye parte sende co munycacyon sayd frende wrytynge wherby yf yt happed yt hys messenger eny synyster fauou borne toward wronge side purposely mangled ye matter mayster shuld oly know treuth also haue occacyon better ware hys messeger ellys myght hape hurte whyle mystake good whan vppon thys delyberacyon taken wyth self wrytte ye mater sente hyt frende thought done mynd full sett reste reste rested long sone yt shewed wrytynge wrytten dyuerse copy one also caried ouer ye se whan remembred shrewd sorte apostatas asse blede parte rone owte religyon rone owte ryghte faythe thought grete parell myght aryse yf su cumpany whych confedered cospyred gether sow ynge settynge forth luther pestylent resyes thys realme shuld maliciously chaunge wordys ye worse put prent booke framed theyre fantesye whych whan wolde afterward reproue shew ye differece myght peraduenture seme coloure cause haue amendede myne vppon syght theyrs eschewyng whereof anow dreuen say thys thyrde busynes publyshyng puttynge boke prynt self whereby theyr etrepryse yf shuld eny intend shall trust preuented frustrate thys haue done myne hed cousayle mo tha one whose aduyce counsayle theyr wysdome lernyng asked byhalf whych haue requeste vouchesaufed rede ouer ye boke ere dyd put yt forth albeit dare suwhat bold comen famylyer maner wt theyr fantesye lyke aske mater eny questyon accordyng ye counceyle saynt poule byddynge v redy gyue rekenyng shew reasonable cause euery man ye faythe hope haue yet make put forth eny boke wherin tretyd eny thyngys wch fayth wolde presume yf better lerned selfe shulde thynke yt eyther profytable lestwyse harmlese whose examinacion iudgment dyd studyously submyte thys worke two thyng specyall amonge dyuerse one lyberall allegacyons messenger wrong parte layd large selfe stode halfe dowt whyther yt couenyent reherse wordys eny ho ly maner sumtyme vnreuerently spoken agaynst goddis holy halows theyre reuerente memoryes tother certayne taly mery word whych mynglid wyth mater su myne owne parte amonge occasyon ell comunycacyon whych albe yt saw none harme yet sumwhat dowted lest shuld vnto sadd men seme ouer lyght waton wayght grauyte erenest matter wherfore two poyntys though hade redy seene esaples ryght holy whych theyre bokys answeryng thobieccions heretiques theyr tyme haue nott letted reherse formall wordys theym whose wrytigis made answere beyng sometyme maner sorte good wold well bere haue also letted wryte mery word ryght ernest worke whych two thyngs could owte godly mennys bokis holy sayntys workys gether good sorte yet mine owne work determyned wold nothyng allow defend iudgement vertuouse cunnynge men wolde eny wyse mysse lyke therefore yt red hyt seuerally sayde theyre aduyce found hyt often happith sum thynge whyche one wyse well lernyd manne wolde haue owte twayne lyke wysdome lernyng specyally wolde haue neyther syde lackyng good probable reasoe theyre parte wherfore syth hyt bycame iudge ouer iudgment theym whome toke chose iudges beyng self hard yt eny man say theym byfore coulde erudyc wytt prudence eny thing preferr could ferther goo lene parte whych ferforth haue folowed lyke wyse dyuerse thyngys put owte chauged theyr good aduyce counsell let nothyng stad boke twayne aduysyd specyally lette stand agaynst eny one eny dowt mouyd contrary thus mych haue thought necessary declaracyon excuse aduertyse shall happen rede thys rude symple work prayeng pacyence pardon god hys especyall grace graunte mych profyte ye redyng pore hart hath mente etendede ye making furst chapyter pthe letter credence sent hys frende trusty secret messenger wyth letter ye authore answeryng ye declara yo ye credence mouth ye messenger whereuppon mater hole worke dependeth pthe letter credence master chauncelour hartely possible ca recomend wythoute thousand thankys good cumpany whan last gether whyche myche yt liked spend sum tyme wyth famylyer comunycacion wherof sum te truste remeber selfe shall better neuer worse shall haue cause haue redy gyue greate thank therfore bolde thys tyme send specyall secrete frende thys berer breke wyth suwhat ferther partely ye matter partely su happed synnys wherof greate spech rumour runneth wherby ye shall haue occasyo legth leysour wyll serue touche certayn dowtes moued synnes mater treated betwene v byfore wheri busynes wold hold goodnes desyre take good time hym yet neuere lesse require hartely leysour serue satysfy full shall longe euer tarye therfore gyue attendaunce vnto dayes howers ye may spare hym tyme whych thing well bestowed consyderynge matter wchynge god well worthy set worldly busynes asyde specyally nede assure folk tal straungely thyngys shall moue onely suche wordis tell yt come fro thense also especially thorough tho casyon letter lewdely wrytte hyther owte londo prest take honeste euer eny man tell wryte shall ye confydence truste yt haue surely take tell forth truth euer ye shal afferme vnto frende sende vnto myche bycause may come selfe beyt therfore bycause longe haue hym talke wt euer ye say reken yt sayde selfe hys trouth secretnes also hys memory wyth comune trust shall mislyke eyther myne affeccyo blyndeth ye shall fynd hym wyse saye better iuge yt mea ly lernyd wythe one thynge addede wherewyth ye wonte well content mery wyt naturre nothynge tonge tayed haue mater beden hym bolde wyth straynynge curtesye wherof cerymonyes dysputacyo marryth mych ye mater whyle one studyeth may behaue shall saye haue say therefore boden hym mynd hys mater hys curtesy frely lay forthe oly thiketh also hym lyst geuyng fote dysputing vnto authorytye born bak wyth reaso thus may ye se bold goodnes put labour busynes send one face owne howse mych bolder chaleg know redy sure defender labour wysdom wel seeth god ye rewarder long preserue pthe lettre author sent wyth boke pryght worshypfull syr moste harty recomendacyon albe yt yt late sent pore mynde ye mouth trusty frend ye desyred letter gyue lesse credence selfe concernynge thyngys brake comuned wt bihalfe yt ye cofydence yt ye haue hym ye wyt lernyng yt founde hym honestye yt moch ye thynk hym yt perceyue beyng wysedom vertu haue hym speryall trust nether ca beleue ye cotrary yt hath comunycacyo made faythfully playne full reporte yet sythe suppose selfe yt yf mought couenyetly cum gether ye wold rather haue chosi haue hard mynde myn owne mouth tha ye mean nother haue sinis fewe day whych haue home put ye mater wrytyng thende ye may hyt mouth frende also whych better y sodenlye one hit mine owne mouthe rede yt yf ye lyste often beste leysure advysydly myne owne penne whych thynge veryly thought selfe mych bounde yt lyked specyall fauour affeccyo towarde greatly regarde esteme myn answere mater yt rumour runig talys countre tolde leters thyther wrytten reason argumet made cotrary shuld lett wyth ande ye wolde ye wrote take thyng vndowted trouth yt shulde frended acertayn surely syr thus poit ye may make selfe sure yt shall neuer wyllingly deceue trust lest might happe yt ouer syght vnware albe yt nothynge sayde vnto frende mouth ryght well enformyd trouth yet mich perceyued hym ye su olke dowted le te many thyngys layd charge onely man ye wrote also luther hym selfe otherwyse coud proued dyd mych therin suffred se shewe hym well ye bokys ye tone tys ye court cocernyng yt tother yt myght myche surely wartaut ye trouth wherin yf ye fynde eny man yet dowteth whether tolde wryte trouth shall yf vnderstand laryne tong fynde ye mean pleasure shall see bokys hym selfe yt neuer full mystrustynge shall fayle fully cotent satysfyed thys warratyse wyll make farforth con erneth eny acte done thyngys reasoned dysputed bytwene v ye coclusyons selfe sure truthes yt dysputable whither reason made beeffectuall insufficyet albe frend eyther trouth thought curtesye sayd accepted good yet wthout preiudyce ye pricipall mater ye may self iuge thus pray take good worthe ye lytle laboure great good wyll hym eny thyng yt may pleasure ye maye vttermost hys lytell power well boldely commaud thus lorde send wt good lady bedfelow hartely well fare ye wolde wysh frende fyrst letter redde whan demau ded hym hys credence shewed ye sent hym eny dowte self many thingis shuld moue vnto dowte ye perceyued many sum folke playne parsuasyo ye cotrary ye wolde glad answere wyth trouthe albe yt thyngys sayd also talked ye wyst well self part ye myght bileue spoke also thether wryten dyuers honest pre y owte londo yt ye wryte many thyngys bor e wrong hand therin sore handelyd forced forswere ab ure certayn herysyes opely put penaunce therfore neuere held eny thys malyce enuye partely freres agaynste whose abusyons preched partly yt preched boldly agaynste pompe pryde inordynate lyuynge mo men speke th preche vsed clargye take gret tokyn shuld meane euyll prose experyence whych men haue yt lyued well good honest vertuouse man farre ambycyon desyre wordly worship chaste humble charytable free lyberall almose dede goodly prechour whose deuowte sermon ye peple greatly edyfyed therfore ye peple say yt thys gere y done onely stoppe menys mouthys put euery sylence yt wold eny thynge speke autys clargy thynk yt none cause also burned poulys crosse new testamet late traunslated eglyshe master wyllyam huchen otherwyse called master tidall say well knowen ere went ouer see ryght good lyuynge studyouse well lerned scrypture dyuerse pl cys englonde well lyked dyd great good wyth prechyng men mutter amonge selfe boke onely fawtlesse also well traunslatyd deuyse burned bycause shuld able proue yt fawtys poules crosse declared haue fou den neuer foude ther dede vntruly surmised yet sum men say fautis traslated dede blame layed awte foud wt thing nothyng worthy onely face ye holy worke thende yt myght seme haue iuste cause burne yt yt none cause kepe owt ye peples knowlege crist gospell goddis law excepte mych onely ye clargye self lyste tha tell v lytle seldom shewed yet y fered well truly tolde watered wt false gloses altered trouthe ye wordis sentence scriptur oly ye mayntenaus theyr authoryte pand fere lest thys thyng shulde euydentely appere people yf suffered rede ye scripture self theyr tong yt thoght ye cause oly whych ye new testamet traslated tidale burned also yt ye clargye thys realme hath bifore thys time costitucion prouyncyall prohybyted eny boke scrypture traunslated englysh tonge ferynge men wyth fyer herytyques whose shulde presume kepe though yt heresie chryste rede cryst gospell pand surely syr quod sum folke yt thynk thys dealyng clargye thus good men myshandlyd declaryng trouth scripture selfe pulled owte ye peples handy leste shulde perceyue trouthe ledde theyre myndys dowte whither luther hi self whose opinion leste whose workys bysynesse bygan wrote dede euyll y borne hande many men therbe thynke neuer mente thingis bycause wrote agaynste thabusyons pardon spake suwhat lyberally agaynste courte rome generally agaynste vycys clargy therfore brought hatered fyrst cyted rome wh n yt forfere bodely harme wyth wrong whereof yt wolde haue bene late loke remedy one burnede vp byfore durste come thether accursed hys bokes dampned vnder great paynis forbodden redd thyng done bycause shulde knowen wronge yt neyther meaneth sayeth odyouse abomynable heresyes people borne hand enduce hatered hi yt wolde aueture appere hys b ki suffered redde pand sey yt mastry make yt seme man shulde herytyque yf may borne hand sayeth thynge whych neuer sayd adueture one lyne taken amonge meny myscostrewed suffering remnante sene wherby yt myghte clerely appere meanyth whych maner delynge man say might lay heresye saynte poule fynde faute saynt iohns gospell yet say worst clargye c ace hereby holde theym selfe content wt codempnyng luther forbyddyng hys bokes ferther abuse ye hatered hys name agaynste euery man y prechynge word god eny thig shulde y wyit playne bolde wythout glose flateryng yf fynde man fauty lett theym lay hys fawte hys charge nedythe call lutherane though luther deuyll yet myght man case say sayeth sum thyng say trew inough neuer ther herytyqu sayd false deuyll hym selfe lyed whe called chryste goddys sonne therefore men thynke name lutherane seruethe clargye comen cloke false crune yt lack specyall mater charge one wyth iugemente laboure bryng hym fyrste infamy name coprysyth make seme cofuted hepe heresyes ca tell pand yet deling wounde theyre owne mater nother way whyle de ame lutherany knowen vertu cunig therby oe ye twayn eyther cause peple yt haue good lyuynge lernyng gret reputacyon thynke yt clargye malice enuy doth vntruly defame el luther doctryne good whyle cunyng men good men lene therto pand therfore yt wysedome call theym lutheranys rather teche holde eny opynions people know luther let yt eyther dy symuled secretly fayr way enduced contrary poynt teche hys nought leste callynge good cunning lutherane may peradueture bryng selfe suspycyone malice nuye luther amonge peple good opynyo thynkyng bygynne doo redy eythere luther sayd euyll y surmysed vppon hym el thyng yt sayth odious seme good inough dede phe sayd also yt yt seemed vnto many men sore thyng farr vnresonable pore symple vnlerned men though fell errours ledde oute ryghte way yt lened thauthoryte byleued vertuouse unyng shuld stede teching bete cruelly wyth abiuracyons opyn shame wyth ell burnyng also yf false wytnesse shall abiuracyo depose yt haue harde hym fall relapse pfynally sayde yt many good well lernyd men thought playnly ye clargye semyth farre owt good order cheryte contrary myldnesse mercyfull mynde theyre er agaynste thesample olde holy father yt cause eny errour wrog opynion faythe eny man one put deth pfor say ye olde holy father vsed dyspute wyth heritiques techyng conuyctynge scrypture fagott way fayth wente well forwarde one heritique turnyd dyd torne many othere abhorre thys crueltie church seme turned think styll thyng dare say thasshes one herytyke spryng vp many make fassyon crystendom seme turned quyte vpp wher crist made infydelis persequutours hys cryste peple su rers make chrysten men persecutours infydelys sufferer wherby thynke secretly christys order yet standeth styll though yt kin perceyued peple take yt styll sequute ye myscrea tys pore peple yt suffer yt vnder false name heretyques trew byleuyng men chrysten martyr pcryst also sey wold neuer haue eny man copelled force vyolece byleue vppon hys fayth wolde men shulde fyght hym hys mater farforthe yt wolde suffer aynt peter fyght hys selfe repreuyd hym strykynge malchus wold defed hi self helyng ere agayn malchus persecutour whych peter smitten geuyng holy body pacyent sufferauce paynefull turmentys hys cruell enmyes wolde put shewed v well hys effectuall ensaumple hys dethe hys godly counceyle hys lyfe confyrmed contynuall pa syo marterdums hys holy martyr hys wyll pleasure shulde myche defende selfe agaynst herytyquys infidelys paganys turkys sarasinys mich lesse tha shuld fyght agaynst theym kyll shulde perseuer setting forth hys fayth agaynst myscreauntis infidellys suche wayes selfe began keepe encreace gotte pacyence su raunce whyche fayth dyuulgate sprede allmost thorow world litle warre fyghting whych way hath thay say well nere redy lost tother way wanne pwhen frend thus declared credes desyred byhalfe hys owne thingys parcas well sayde take dede mind whome ye wold fayne answere satysfye wyth resone ye trustyd better able myne aswer neyther mind opynyon hym whych dyd wold thyng stand abyde fayth byleue cryst catholyk chyrche suche tys thys mater concernyd eny parte beleue dealig thys worlde iustyce vniustyce sum spyrytuall personys pursuyng condempnyng heretyquys theyr werkys heresyes thought sayd hym selfe myght wtoute eny parell heresy theyr owne parte notwt standyng eny mannes iudgemet geuin yet well resonably dowt ther though thought heresy thynke thopynyons eny man good catholyque whych herisyes dede yet might thought wythout eny parell heresy dowte whether herytyke mannys iudgment codempned one syth myght well happe neuer held opinion put vppon hym eyther fals deposycyons wrong full wytnes error malyce vniust iudges condempnyd sometyme percase ignorauce som iudges wold codemne heresye artycles wyser better lernyd wold poynt iudgment alow good catholyque tother iudgment decerne iudge contrary phow yt sayd ye lernyng specyall trust co fydens thigys euer ye herd shuld elli ye fully determynyd gyue full credece take ye trouth answere shuld brig wherei ye ryght hartely desired take paine ye myght mater hys mouth know mynde large pafter thys made eny aswere hys wordys demaunded maner acquayntaunce bytwene hym theruppon perceyuyng hym haue sone scole enqueryng farther hym faculte geuyn study vnderstode hym haue geuyn dylygece latyn tonge facultyes rought tolde merily logyk rekenyd babelyng musyke serue syngers arythmetryk mete merchaut geometry mason astronomy good man phylosophy ye vanyte yt logyk lost good deuynyte wyth ye subteltyes theyre questyons babelyng theyre dyspycyons byldyng vppon reason whych rather geuith blyndnes tha light sayd hath lyght holy scripture therfore sayde biside latyne tonge ben whych mych comende studiouse holy scripture whych sayed lernyng nough crystyn man wyth thapposteles held self cotent therin saide labored onely many textys therof hart also enserche sentence vnderstandyng therof ferre myght perceyue hym selfe interpretours tolde neyther hys tyme wolde well serue hym rede also founde great swetnes texte selfe coulde fynde harte lese eny tyme glosi towchyng eny defycultye said founde experience beste surest interpretacio ley conferre one texte wyth whych ayle amonge theym well sufficiently declare theim self thys waye sayde vsyde whych founde sufficient surest shulde surely tary yt founden owte lernyd mane owne laboure said euery able inough wyth helpe god whych neuer faylith theym faythfully truste hys myse hath promysid seke shall fynde knocke shall haue openyde v shalbe openid booke seynt iohn saith thapocalips shytt wyth vii clap openyd lambe whan shetteth ca open whan openyth man shytt puppo wordys lyke whan consyderyde youre frend studiouse scrypture though haue goode opynyon hym tyme hade contrary yet playne wt reason set mater well lustely forward put somwhat dowte whether yong scolers sutime ne new fantesyes fallen luther secte ye peradueture suwhat feryng dyd good mynde rather sende hym wyth message ye trustyd shuld sumwhat aswered satysfied therfore thought metely many mater wegh make hym vnaduysed answere wyth good wordys welcomyng time ptedyng lake leysour psent bisines requyred retorne morow whych tyme wold order myne affares wold haue conference gether hys erande length wyse beyng departyde beganne gather mynde hole effecte rememberaunce wolde serue purposyd bycause wolde haue yt redy myne eye myght fully effectually answere leuyng parte vntouchyd suche order hade purposyd yt wytt maner haue aboue rehersyd bryefely commyttyd yt wrytynge pthe second chapyter p sumaryly declared order author intendyth trete matter purposyd vnto hym wherof fyrst oppynyon conceyued mennys heddes certayn parsolate abiured heresy preching pilgrymagys ymagis prayer made saynt therin greately wronged ye author breuely declareth hys mynde concernyng confutacyon perylouse pernycyouse opy yons morow whan cu men agayne sumwhat vii clocke appoynted hym takyng hym wyth stody saruantys warned yf shulde happen desyre speke wyth certayne excepte whome gaue theym knowlege shulde dy erre theym tyll nother leysor sett hym downe wyth litle table shewed vnto hym purposed byhalf short wordys many long thyng wherof rehersall losse tyme hym well knew theym redy wolde su iuous recapytulacyon sett aparte brefely conuenyently coulde shew hym mynde theym fyrst bygyn bygan abiuracyon man spake secudly wold touche condempnacyon burnyng ye new testament traunslated tyndale thyrdly sumwhat wold speke luther hys secte generall forthly fynally ye thyng touched laste wytt wart fyghtyng agaynst infydelys wyth condemnacyo heretyques vnto deth whych twoo poynty hym selfe combyned knytte gether pand fyrst touchyng mater mannes ab racyon reported spyrytualtye dyd hym wrong make seme lykly layed theym displeasure malice toward hym peech ng ye say quod agaynst theyer vycyouse lyuyng hym tother syde alegyd myche connyng vertue goodnes wyll neyther enter prayse theym dyspreyse hym wherein standyth nothyng theffecte thys mater e dyd wold passe ouer su parte therof shortely pbut thys mater though hole spyrytualtye wherin man dowtith ryght vertuous godly man theyre lyuyng farr wors deuyll yet yf wrong hath matter man agaynst eny caus coplayn ouer thys yf man hys lyuynge innocent saynt yet yf infected fautye herysyes thys matter wrong yet besyde thys yf onely thyng vertuous also thoese heresyes whereof detected vtterly clene fautles yet yf suffycyent wytnes neuer fals dede seming honest lykely say trew prouyd opyn courte fauty ther albeyt suche case hys wytnessys wronged hym yet hys iudges done hym ryght therfore letting passe say praysse dysprayse either hys iudg thyngys impertinent point shew yt onely dyd hym wrong also shewed hym mynd gretest fauour vsed toward hym charytable rcy yt euer wy vsyd eny man uch case fyrst wron yt hys iudgi hy mer ell wher report yt could assygn yf ny done must n haue ben one twoo thyngys eyther vntruly iudgyd haue pchyd artycles detectyd pchyd none dede ellys sum artycles prechyd iudeged condemned heresyes none dede excepte man wolde say though proued conuyctyd heresye yet shuld haue bene put penaunce ellys poynt eny thynk shall speke fourth parte shall towch generall ordre chyrche takyth condemnacyon herytyques tother poyntys fyrst eny preest wrote owte londo cuntraye eny artycle hys prechyng hys iudeges declared herysy dede good ageynst fayth crystys chyrch lett hym name artycle eyther ye shall fynde shall name man charged wyth ellys shall ye fynde yt shall name dede selfe shall pceyue heresyes ere artycles wyth chargede yt shuld worshyppe eny ymages pray enyseyntys go pylgrymagys whyth thyngys suppose euery good crystyn man wyll agre heresyes therfore shall lett poynt passe resort secund se well prouy preched syr quod end wold parte well agree theym rysys yet haue ha thy wold therfore w herysye well tell ythse men wold e yf myghte hard tyffly say nay whych hold theyre pea bere theym selfe full coldely wold take ye therfore saye quod youre frende may sure thyngys whan pageantys played towne remeber worke haue hard lempster kyng father dayes ye pryour brought preuyly strauge weche ito ye chyrch yt sayd sent euer hard man ley ue myracles done pylgrymagys vncertayn wroght rather proue shulde goddes myracles deuyllys wonder xviii chapiter pthe author dyfferreth thanswere forsayde obieccyons fyrst scrypture proueth yt ye chyrche chryste erre eny necessary artycle chrystys fayth thys chapyter bee wordys cryst specyally touched su cathedram moysi sederut c que dicut vobis facite que autem faciunt nolite facere cocernyng authoryte chyrch suerly quod parte ca good thak ye haue fayntely defendyd youre parte though yt corruptyd aduocate yt wold colusyon hadell hys clyent mater feebly pleasure hys aduersary ye haue sayd therin ca tell whe mych man may say certenly suppose mich ye eyther haue hard man say ca self say ye lest wyse much haue hard el coud haue sayd self vndowtyd ye spake shotyng begynnig thys gere nere goeth pryk shall see thys promyse yt wold fayn bere ouer yt myght hold bidden well ab e prouyd trew trust ue yt fals shote quite gon suerte yt coud reke fayth cristendome cum poynte syth yt agreed redy betwene v ymagys pylgrymagys myracles bene eyther shewyd god comprobacyon hys plesure theryn woders wrought dyuyll oure delusyon dampnacyon may eyther appere v yt done dyuell wyll yt well folow yt done god yf prouyd done god good hys chirch wyll clere ynough wonder wrought dyuell dysceyt crysten peple syth eyther partyes prouyd implyeth reprofe purpose wyll assay shew trust ryght well proue trouth syde sum one way paradueture y wete aswell prouyng god doth myracles reprouing confutyng yt shuld done dyuell furst wold fayne mete wyth obieccyons answer forthwyth whyle fresh sauyng semith better whyle differ forasmuch sum thyng therbe wheruppon wyll requisyte yt furst agreed wythout whych lyke walke wyde wordys ronne ryot lose mater could nother haue ground order ende pnow yf wer thys mater dyspute wt paynym wolde make questyon betw ne theyr myracles albeyt shuld haue clere mater thend yet must nedys longe mater much entryked yt shuld cu thend hole bokys wold yt hold confutyng theyrs vnto thassertacyo specyally receyue oure scrypture betwene v nothyng comune groud vppon reason yf shoulde dyspute wt iew lesse labour shuld haue syth shulde haue wt hym thogh deny new testamente yet reson ye old testament agreed vppo wherin shuld ary text ye sentence vnderstanding therein shulde haue hym styfly wythstande v pbut syth wee shall mater dyspute reason wyth agree theym selfe crysten menne oure dyspycyons y much shorter muste nedys aggree gether moo thyngy wee muste agree reason fayth refusyth yt ouer wee shall agree vppon hole corpus scrypture aswell new testament olde interpretacyon wee maye paraduenture stykke yt pyes quod pwell quod y thynge wherein ye thynke wee shall vary interpretacyo scrypture pnot remember quod except scrypture yt self wheruppo talk worshyppyng ymag prayeng sayntys whych men thynke greate questyon yf scrypture well interpretyd p ye q agre thyngys arn cyonyd gospell spokyn cryst vnto saynt peter hys apostels dyscyples sayd self onely selfe theyer successours crystys flok v y wete euery man shall appertayne hys parte pwhereby mene q pi mene quod esample wha sayd nisi abundauerit iusticia vestra plusquam scribaru phariseo rum non intrabitis regnu celo rum except iustyce abound excede ye iustyce scrybys pharesyes ye shall neuer cu heuyn saith thou wylt enter kyngdome heuyn kepe comaundementys dyd say thyngys theym crystyn men yt shuld come pi thynke yes quod seconde word concernyng comaudment furst theyr iustyce shulde better iustyce scrybys pharesyes paraduenture spake specyally hys appostels self yt shuld lyke ye scrybys pharesyes whych comaundyd many thyngys dyd nothyng theym selfe pthat y mynde quod well taken doth holy saynt augustyne expoune syth ye think sayd word hys appostels specyally rather hys hole flok whether thik sayd yt onely el also yt shuld come theyr placis succede offyce pnay god q ye byshoppys sayd yt prelat spyrytuall ruler hys chirch yt euer shalbe ye chyrch forbyddyng binde lay vppon pore mennys bakk importunable burdeyns bering wherof self wyll onys put forth fynger puery well sayd q thynke sayd ye suche thyngys byd ye se pin wold lord quod yt people shuld prelatys shuld comaud far comaundyd lawe god mente therfore sayed sat vppon ye chayr moyses wyllyd shuld ye cause obeyd therin ment thyngys onely shuld comaund god commaundyd people law gyuen vnto moyses crystyn men lykewise shall obey byshoppys prelatys commaundynge onely suche thyngys hym self hath comaundyd hys people hys gospell hys owne law pand nothyng el q meanyth yt lorde parable samarytane beryng ye woudyd ye inne hys church delyueryng hym hoste hym self dressyd hys wound wythe wyne oyle lef e wyth hoste ii grotys two testame tys promysyd hoste besyde ye euer hoste wolde bestowe vppon wold cam agayn recompense hym therfore also place spake sauyour sayd scrybys pharesyes besyde ye law moyses whose sete satt dyd lay greate fardellys faste bounde mennys bakkis beryng wherof wold moue fynger self yet bad peple theyr prelatys wold byd though burden heuy let yt though shuld se bydders clene contrary whych addyd pby oure lady q lyke thys glose yt makyth bo dy law church bynde v tha ye iewes almost wyth moyses lawe wote well cryst sayd cum ye ouerchargyd shall refreshe hys appostels sayd bare lawe moyses beside ceremony set scrybys pharesyes euer theye able bere fulfyll therefore cryst ca call v law liberte yt takyng away bande wery ceremoniall lawes therfore sayth sauyour law yt callyth v vnto yoke saythe y fyt easy burdeyn lyght wherby yt apperyth met gouernaunce hys people bee hardnes dyffyculte kepyng thyng lyke lawes moyses thereof durst nede make self iudge yf ye bethynk well wene ye thys age chose yow wold rather bounden many ye lawes crystys heresyes spycyng theyre prechyng wyth rebukynge preesthod prelacye people pleasure turne many man ruyne theym selfe also hen dyuell dysseyuyth theyre blynde affeccyons pthey take good zele people theyre malycyous enuy great vertew theyre ardente appetyte preche wherin haue gret pryde people prayse prech wene wold thogh god wold hys mouth comaund cotrary pwhy shuld ye wene quod whereby ye sure saythe dominus autem intuetur cor onely god beholdyth harte therfore sayth sauyouriuge time pi iuge quod vppon ope thing well apparant speke whose erronyous oppynyons theyr prechyng ad theyr obstynate mayntenaunce theyr dysobedience haue amendyd mater wyth heresy boldly stubburnly defendyng syth connynge preche theye god bounden preche man law made coud made authoryte forbede theym thys thought suffycyencly uyd word thappostell oportet magi obedire deo quam hominibus though appostels specyally sent god preche heresy sow sedycyon amonge crysten men appostels dede sente comaundyd god preche fayth iewes one thys sort thys new kynde prechers beinge demaundyd yt vsyd say hys sermon day men prechyd well gospell answered thought saw prechers parsecutyd stryfe bysynes aryse vppo theyr prechig whych thyngys sayd ad wrote frute gospell cryste sayd non vem pacem mittere sed gladium come send peace worlde sword thys worshypfull vnderstandynge yt cryste wolde make deuision among infidel remanaunt wynne therfore appostels wolde sow cocle dyssension among ye cristen people chyste might lese som frute strife amonge herers parsecucio precher cannot lightly grow among crysten menne prechinge straunge newelties bringynge vp new fa gell heresy infeccio olde faythe pone wyst hys partinacie oppynio yt wold might bouden preche prohibicyon wythstandynge aftere dyuers bolde open defece thereof laste folk honorable fewe reasoned withall onely lawe shewed hym contrary hys oppynion whych law made generall coucell also playne authoryte holye scrypture prouyd hys oppinion erronyous parceyued hym selfe satysfyed yt mekely knolegyd hys errour offryd abiure submyt hymself penaunce morow cam forth open presece peple saw many oft hard hym preche hys secrete pryde fell open passion shame shulde heere hym go bak wyth hys worde whych hys sermon grete estymacyo fyrst syghte people reuokyd hys reuocacion sayd alowd myghte well harde yt hys oppynyon trewe yt day beefore deceyuyd confessyd yt false thus held hys stubburnly wythout reason tyll bookys shewyd hym agayn self red people parceyuyd audyence stode hym feele vnderstand hys proude foly defence hys indefensyble erroure theruppon last yelded hym selfe agayne suche secret pryde oure gostely enemy conueyd harte hym whych ensure semyd hys outward maner meke symple soule manne shuld haue sene somers day let wyth lye pariury defed self stande defece theyre errours false denyenge theyr owne dede theyr great parell fyre yf theyre iudges nott marcyfull theyre malyce deseruyth thys ne selfe doth last cofesse thynke yf theye abiure theye shall suffred preche agayn scabbyd ych vayn glory catch theyr prechynge though world worse yt theyre lyfe lye theron yet wold log pulpetyd thys saye hathe comen su haue wyth contempt lernyng geuen scrypture alone whose affeccyons pryde slouth hath begynnyng bene parceyuid selfe haue accomptyd theyr vycys deuocyon pwold ye quod condempne maner study whych man hathe gret affeccyon ye scripture alone delyte therof felyth lytle sauoure thyng l shuld lese tyme phylosophy mother heresyes let scrypture alone pnaye quod mynde neuer thyng wryten thys worlde canne wyse coparable wyth parte holy scripture yet thynke lyberall scyence gyfte god also cast away worthy wayte ad handemaydys gyue attendauce vppon diuinite diuinyte rek best parte coteynyd holy scripture thys say shall haue time thereto fro youth entendeth churche ward make self wyth goddys help met thoffyce precher beyt ny man eyther happe begyn late yt shall paraduentu e haue tyme therto el youth haue affeccyons vsynge greate moderacyon temperaunce prechynge men thynge flee desyre prayse shew conyng euer mystrustyng hys owne inclynacyons lyue drede feare dyuyllis subtell sleyghte inuencions though lye contynuall awayt vppon euery prechour cach hym pryde yf yet hys hyest enterpryse proudyst tryumph standyth ye bryngyng abuse thynge yt y hys nature ye best therfore gret labour makyth grete bost wyth tone tother next grace helpe god gote wt abstynes prayour clenes lyuig afore thing necessary come well surely enstructyd poyntys artycles ye church beleuyth whych thyngys onys fyrmly ad fastely trouth eny poynt fayth se profe many thyng naturall wherof reaso ca attayn cause artycle fayth styll eny power ye reason hath perceyue cause shall iuge impossible proue trew byleue eye better wytt table stone x comaundementys put remeberaunce agayne certeyne coclusyons law nature theyre reason ouerwhelmed wyth sensualytye forgotten thende shuld kepe bihest ye better gaue theym greate hepe lawes cerymoneys moo kepe theym strayte strayynge abrode ryot wroughte greate wonder theye shulde well se thyngys hys owne deede wherby myght haue ye drede transgresse wrytyng gaue warnyng also cryst god wolde onys send spryngyng themself shuld gyue herynge stede moyses also well patryarkes prophetys fygures prophesyes god ceaced wise foreshew hys cummyng hys cause hys lyuyng hys deyng hys resurreccyon hys holy actys yf pryde enuy lettyd fygurys ad prophysyes sett comparyd wyth hys cummyng conuersacyon doyngys myghte well haue made iewes know hym parceyuyng good vnderstandyng lawe wryten sent alway sum good men whose wordys well lyuyng sumtyme also manyfeste myracles shewed therwyth neuer left destytute suffycyent knolege logyd lern lawe plete glory dyspute itt teche ytt agayne mekely mannys fraylte could suffer specyally fulfyll kepe pyet thys whe world decay ruyne vertew ca sauyour cryste redeme v wt hys deth leue v hys new law wherof long prophecied prophete hyeromy lo day comyng sayth lord wha shall order dyspose house israell ye house iuda new couenaut testament shall gyue law theyre myndys shall wryte yt theyr hart wylbe theyr lord shalbe people thys law wryte menys hartys accordyng ye wordys phet fu st broght sauyour ye house israell ye house iuda hym self sayth specyally sent set sayth lorde vnto ye shepe yt peryshyd house israell also sayd y good take ye brede fro ye borde ye chyldern cast yt dogg yet onely redy towardnes sum caus partetakers ye brede also sone ye stubbernes obstynate infydelyte ye iewes causyd seynt poule thappostels say vnto face gospell crist ordenyd god furst prechyd vnto syth yt ye refuse yt lo depart fro gentylys theyr stede chyrch gatheryd world abrode whych wythstandyng tyme ye iewes couertyd made many good crysten man manye ye peple turnyd vnto cryst syns conclusyo tyme shall cu whe ye remnaut yt shalbe lefte shall saue selfe faythe thys y callyd law crystis fayth law hys holye gospell mene onely wordys wryten bokys euangelistys mych specyally ye substaunce fayth yt self whych lorde sayd wolde wryte mennys hartys onely secrete operacyon god hys holy spyryte iustyfyeg good cryste ether workig manys good wyll feccyon fayth soule wyth good intent offerer secret infusyon vertew soule innocet infant also yt furst wythout wryting reueled heuenly mysteryes hys blessed mouth thorow erys hys apostels dyscyples theyr holy hartys lyke maner furst wythowt wrytyng onely wordys prechyng spredde yt abrode world hys faythe mouthys hys holy messenger put menys erys hys holy hande wryten mennys hartys euer eny worde thereof almoste wrytten boke conuenyet law lyfe rather wryten lyuely myndys men dede skynnys bestys nothynge dowt ytt beene neuer gospell bene wrytten yet shoulde substaunce thys faythe neuer haue fallen oute chrysten folkys hartys spyryte plantyde yt shulde haue wateryd shulde haue kepte yt shoulde haue encreased yt pbut hath yt lyked oure lorde hys hye wysdome prouyde dyscyples haue writen many thingys holy lyfe doctryne fayth yet farre saynt iohn sayth worlde coude haue comprehen hyd pthese bokis ar tempryd secrete coucell holy gost playn symple euery man may fynd theym may parceyue reson therof farr beter vnderstode bok thogh myghte happely textys whych yet necessyte parceyue yet poynt theyr fayth warnyd texte myghte constrewyd contrary theyr fayth pand none euagelyst none appostle wrytyng euer sent fayth eny nacyon yf furst enformyd worde god begon church place pand parte wolde lytyll dout euangelystys appostels bothe many gret secrete mysteryes spake much openly much playnely mouth amog peple euer put yt wrytyng much theyr wrytyngys lykly ynough tyme come handy paganys paynyms hoggys dogg metely haue precyous perlys put vppon theyre nose holy foode dashyd theyre self blyndyd theyr wylfully wynkyng eye hydyng puttyng vp agayn iewell yt began brynge forth shew bryght lustre whero theyr bleryd eye myght endure old pand maruell thogh thappostels thus theyr speche yt therfore cryste sayd dyscyples haue say ye able bere yt yet whyche onys apperyd tyme vppon ye dysclosyng grete mystery holy sacrament holy flesh hys body herers sayd abyde thys harde worde therwt secrete mystery lyeth yet coueryd cocernynge comyng antecryste ye day maner fassyon fynall iudgement whyche shall neuer fully dysclosyd tyll tymys appoyntyd goddys hye prouydence mete conuenient tyme tyme yt lykyth hys maieste haue thyngys knowen done hys chyrche y yt dout temperyth hys reuelacyos wyse doth insumate inspyre brestys hys crysten people secrete instynct holy gost consent agre gether chaunge sure holy goste god sent hys chyrch cryste hym self hath promisyd vnto thende world perseuer abyde hys church shall neuer suffer hys catholyk chyrch neyther agree makynge law shalbe god shulde mysseconstruccyo scrypture bryng vp beleue cryste one god egall wyth hys father wyth ye holy goste yf ye trouth otherwyse dede therefore syth chyrche whych cryste y assystente hys holy spyryte fayth taught mouth textys semyd contrary contrary dede therwyth declaryd textys ye ryght vnderstadyng pand albeyt yt sauyour shewyd playnly prouyd yt scrypture geuen good token suffycyent knowlege hym yet thentent shulde well know hys word ordynaunce nedyth none othere authoryte hym self y beleuyd obeyd wryten wryten sum thyngys dyd therfore byd su thyngys also beleuyd wherof haue holy scripture whan gospell spekyth onely wy e durst thys world haue bene bold ut eny thing el therto whe ye gospell spekyth wine onely tornyd hys precyous blood man wold adue ture make myxture water y ye chyrch way trew fals tha prechers thys chyrche sholde preche teche v better yt chyrch yf yt haue prechours pyt hath quod som preche som tyme ye wyll suffre theym ye punysshe theym burne pnay quod wyser tha yll burned v wyll rather swere boke yt neuer sayd ellys wyll say thys appereth suche secrete vnknowen chyrche cryst hauyng opynyons ye chyrche ye chyrch hath euer hath abyde theyr fayth theyr prechynge wold neuer go backe wyth goddys worde dye therfore thys chyrch take chyrch heretyques haue many suche martryris therin ye byleued agaynst opynyons appereth hystoryes many theyr bokes secrete chyrche neuer yet foude herde eny one lyfe wolde forswere faythe saue hys lyfe also preestys bysshops must haue yf chyrch cryst chyrch haue none ye ech vnknowe though suche chyrches haue false opynyo euery preest euery woman yet thys heresye false wyl serue vnknowen chyrch ye holder opynyon put man may take vpon hym preche medle preest tyll chosen congregacyon thys gynary chyrch whych n know h hand pwel quod shall se sone whan come therto bu present purpose yt perceyued harme people toke translacyon prologys glosys wyclyff also hym holpe set forth hys secte tha ye cause myche yt y daungerouse translate texte scrypture oute one tonge nother holy saynt hierom testyfyeth myche traslacio hard alwai kepe ye sentence hole yt saye causys counsayle holden oxenford prouyded vppon grete payn shold fro thense forth translate th nglysh toge eny langage hys authoryte waye boke lybell tretyce man openly secretly eny boke lybel tretyce rede newly made tyme sayde iohan wyclyffe synnys yt sholde made eny tyme tyll translacyo dyocesane yf nede sholde requyre prouyncyall counsayl approued thys y law yt many long haue spoke haue al ye whyle rought seke whyther say trouth trow yt thys law ye se thig vnreasonable yt neyther forbedeth ye traslacios red yt redy well done old byfore wyclyffys dayes dapneth hys bycause yt new bycause yt noughte prohybyteth new made prouydeth yt shall redde yf mysse made tyll good examinacio ameded excepte traslacios wyclyf made tidal yt ye malicyo mynd ye traslator wyse hadled labor lost go med pi longe trouth quod euen syt thornes tyll se constytucyo self euery ellys hath euer take yt far otherwyse euer haue herd spoke therof tyll surely wyll se yt selfe ere slepe pye shall soner eased q suffer se syt longe thornes therfore ye shal se yt pand therwyth fet hym forthe constytucyons prouyncyall wyth lynwood thervppon tornyd hym place ye tytle de magistris whan hym selfe redde sayde maruayled mich happened playne mater men far abused reporte yt farre wronge p thys groweth quod partely malyce partely slouthe neglygence ye folke glad byleue tell forth thynge maye sowne dysprayse clergye tha serche sure whyther say trewe pthe xv chapyter pthe messenger moueth agaynst ye clergye yt thoughe haue made law therof yet wyll dede suffer non englysh byble man hand vse burne theym fynde theym somtyme burne man ensample layeth one rychard hune shewyng chauceler londo murdered hym pryson hanged hym faynyng yt hanged hym self codempned hym heresye bycause englyshe byble burned byble hym together wherunto ye author aswereth suppose quod thys opynyon rather growen another way y wytte reason yt clergye though law serue therfore yet dede take tra slacyons euery lay mann hand sometyme wyth burned couycted heresye burne ye englysh byble wythout respecte ye translacyon olde new bad good pforsoth quod yf thys tha yt mynde well done byleue ye mystake yt howe yt ye haue sene saye selfe haue sene shew byblys fayre olde wryten englyshe whyche haue ben knowen sene byshop dyocyse lefte laye mennys handy woman suche knewe good catholyke folk vsed yt wyth deuocyon sobernes trouth suche founden handy heretyques vse take awaye cawse none burned farre euer cowlde wytte onely founde fawtye wher many set forth wyth euyll prologys glosys malycyously made wyclyf heretykes good wold wene mad burne vp ye byble wheri foud faut law yt letted yt loked red pmary quod haue herd good men say euen london many yerys agoo dayes bysshop last dyed burned vp fayre bybles englysh eny man hathe lyghly sene therto fautlesse awght eny man cowlde fynde eny byble y laten yet bysydys thys burned vppe dede bodye man hym selfe whome theym selfe hadde hanged byshoppys pryson makyng though ye man haged hymselfe burnynge hys body colour onely bycause founde englysshe bybles hys howse wherin neuer founde faut bycause englyssh pwho tolde thys tale quod pforsothe dyuers honest quod saw yt specyall one saw man hangyng ye bysshops pryson ere cutte downe told yt yt well clerely proued yt chaunceler hys kepers kylled man fyrst tha hanged hym layd heresye hym hatred yt sued pmunyre agaist dyuers person suyt taken mortuary audyence archebysshop caterbury tha proued heresye nothynge ellys possessyon good englysh byble vppon heresye proued agaynst hym whome hanged lest sholde saye hym selfe burned vppe holy scrypture god body good man therwyth haue herd hym called honest person good substaunce pforsothe quod good substaunce thynke well worthe markys hys worldly conuersacyon among peple haue herd non harme surely towchynge hys fayth towarde cryste thynketh may bold say honest touching trouth word yt hath tolde thys tale honeste dede thynketh ye take hym pwhy q ye know ye mater well pforsoth q wel know fro top yt suppose ther many yt know yt mych better haue ben dyuers tymes present selfe certayn examynacyons therof haue also dyuers many tymes sunderly talked wyth almost except ded hym self moost knew mater whych mater many tymes sundry placys examyned specyally baynardys castell one day yt examyned great length long tyme euery beyng sent byfore redy yt could founden yt eny thyng could tell yt sayd could eny thyng tell mater thys examynacyo byfore dyuers grete lordys spyrytual temporall kyngys honorable counsayll sente thyther hyghnesse nonys hys blyssed zele pryncely desyre borne serchynge trouthe whervnto hys gracyous mynde myche enclyned ben ryghte honorable enformed one shewed frend hys yt could go take hym sleue yt kylled hune rychard hune hys name whome ye speke also self psent iudgement gyue powlys wher vppon hys bokys hys body burned thyngys well knowe ye haue h rd thys mater hath tolde talys far ye trouth pin good fayth q frende tolde one thynge yt ye speke nowe one sayde cowlde go take hym sleue kylled hunne dyd dede byfore lordys came euen chaunceler sayd lordys thys y wha asked knew cofessed yt yt suche vnlawfull craft take profe thei say necromacie bysshops yt wolde haue man burned wychecrafte told also yt nother whyche sene meny men yt hanged self man long offyce vnder dyuers kyngys almoygners ye goody men kylled self appoynted ye law hys offyce deodandes gyuen almoyse man haue herd saye shewed vnto lordys suche experyence good playne toke whych perceyued well hunne dyd neuer hange hym selfe haue herd also spyrytuall man one loued well chaunceler laborer parte yet coulde deny lordys hadde tolde temporall man frende hys hunne neuer ben accused heresye yf neuer sued premunyre saynt mary shrewd worde yt dede yt went nere mater tother two thyngys dyd p yes good faythe quod thre lyke nere whan herd trouth many thyngys layd vppon herynge semed myche suspycyouse whyche yet whan answered alway loste halfe theyr strength thre mater promyse proued tryfles yf ye herd theym ye wolde haue lawghed theym seuen yere p beseche quod lette howe proued p lothe quod lette lese youre tyme suche tryfles yt sythe ye longe sore therfore rather ye sh lde lese youre chylde theym ye shall haue theym thre shortely fyrste ye muste vnderstande bycawse comynge together lordys grenewych baynard castell tryenge oute mater sholde frustrate suche dylygence done euery man aughte hadde sayde therin redy agaynste theyre co mynge began wyth fyrste poynte ye spake specyall mocyon whervppon kyngys hyghnesse sent theym thyther wherfore rehersall made cause theyr comyng grettest temporal lord present sayd vnto certayn seruaut hys stadyng bysyde syr ye told ye one shewed could go take hym ye sleue yt kylled hune haue ye brought hym hyther syr q yf yt lyke lordshyp man yt told poyntyng one caused come thither lord asked man howe saye ye syr ye ye sayd ye coulde forsothe lorde quod yt lyke youre lordsshyp sayd myche thys gentylman dyd somwhat mys e take dede tolde hym neyghbour tolde cowlde yt y neyghboure quod lorde thys man syr quod bryngynge forthe one whyche also warned asked whyther sayd could yt nay forsothe quod lorde sayde cowlde yt self sayde one told could yt well q lord tolde forsothe lorde quod neyghbour tha ye askyd syr knowe one tell kylled hunne forsoth quod yt lyke lordshyppe sayd knew one surely yt could tell h kylled hym sayd dede th knowe one whyche thought veryly coulde tell kylled hym well quod lord last yet wyth mych worke come sowhat wherby thyn yt tel nay forsoth lorde q yt woma wolde wt lordshyppis well q lord woman man one shall hadde euer fayth lord q wt wold tell woders god haue wyst tell many maruylouse thyng ere q ye lordis haue herd tolde h lord quod yf thynge h bene stolen wold haue tolde h yt therfore thike could well tell kyld hunne stale horse surely sayd lordys thynke trow could tell yt deuyll nay trouth trow quod could neuer se vse eny worse waye lokyng onys hande therwyth lordys laughed asked forsoth lord quod egyp yan lodged euen lambeth y gone ouer see nowe trow countre yet saye yt y grete waye hense wente ouer lytell moneth ago pnow forsoth q frende thys processe came wyse purpose gret post well thywted puddyng pryk pray poynt came second mater hym th ben offyce vnder many kyngys almoygners knew hys owne experyece ued hune h hanged hym selfe pforsoth q called nexte asked wherby knewe yt wold god ye sene contenauce lykelyhed sayd suwhat far myche amased loked though hys eyen wolde haue fallen oute hys hed lordys lappys ye questyo answered sayd yt saw well sawe hym ere take q ye lordys dyd many mo whych yet vppon syght could tel lordys quod haue nother syght insuche thyng tha men haue syghte quod forsoth q yt y vnknowen yt haue occupyed grete whyle vnder dyuers ye kyngys almoygnyers haue sene consydered many haue hanged self therby yf se one hange tell anon whyther hanged hym self toke tell quod lordys forsothe quod tell ye toke perceyue yt well ynoughe myn owne syghte whan herd hym speke hys owne syghte therwyth saw syght lokynge thoughe hys eyen wold haue fallen theyr lapp coulde fewe forbere laughynge sayd se wel surely ye haue syghte selfe sayde one lorde meryly peraduenture om cunyng experyece iewels perceyue hys owne eye er stone ryghte counterf te though well make nother man perceyue token thys good felowe thowghe tell v markys yet hath suche experyence hangyng hymselfe perceyueth vppon syght whyther man hanged hym selfe ye forsothe lorde quod euer lordysshyp sayth knowe yt wel ynough selfe haue sene many reason myn offyce quod nother lorde meryly offyce hathe experyence hangyng hath hange yet tell naye syr q yt lyke lordshyp medleth wyth theym hange theym selfe well q one lordys many haue ye medled wyth youre dayes wyth many lorde quod haue ben offycer vnder two almoygners therfore haue sene many howe many quod one lordys tell quod howe many wote well haue seene many haue ye sene quod one hundred naye quod hundred haue ye sene foure score ten therat lytell studyed one standynge doute loth lye laste sayd thoughte nay fully foure score ten asked whither hath sene twenty therto wythout eny styckynge answered nay twenty therat ye lordys lawhged well se sure sene twentye dout whyther sene four score ten asked ther sene xv therto sayd shortely nay lykewyse ten laste came fyue fro fyue foure bygan studye agayn tha cam thre tha shame fayn say yt sene many mo wha asked wha place necestyte draue last vnto trouth wherby yt appered neuer sene one hys lyfe yrysh felow called croke shank whome hadde sene hangynge olde bar e wha hys connyng come thys bad walke lyke hym self one sayd vnto hym bycawse yet conynge ynoughe crafte hangynge pytye hadde experyence therof one mo p forsothe q youre frende thys mad felowe came ye thyrd tale wyse poynt pye shall quod temporal man reported yt vpo ye mouth spyrytual good worshypfull man hys trouthe worshyp grete credyte surely spyrytuall man man worshyp also wel knowe co nyng vertuouse therfore ye lord myche meruayled knowig suche shold lyke fynde eyther tone tother eyther make vntrewe reporte vntrewly denye ye trouth fyrst temporall lordys heryng spyrytuall person sta dyng sayd lordys helpe god halydom mayster doctour sayd vnto hys owne mouth yf hune sued premunyre shold neuer haue accused heresye say master doctour quod lordys ye trewe ellys sayd ye surely lordys quod sayd thyng thys sayd dede yf hune accused heresye wold neuer haue sued premunyre lo lordys q tother gladde ye fynde true man wyll ye commaunde eny seruyce nay trouth q one ye lord mater wyl ye maye go whan ye wyll haue espyed good yt word l one yt maketh mater whyche waye stand one horse myl myll horse dike ere ye go go e e ye drynke naye lordys quod h wyll drynke dod yelde therwyth made curteyse wet hys waye leuynge lordys lawghynge se good playne olde honest man contrary theyr two talys yet wha herd agayne marked dyfference bytwene theym toke theym bothe one bycause ye wordys one trouthe q frend thre thyngys came meryly passe wold good thynge herd theym may man se mysse vnderstandynge maketh mysse reportyng tale eeth thorowe many mouthes catcheth many new fethers whyche whan pulled away agayne leue hym pylled coote somtyme bare byrdys ar thyn e veryly thys grete euydence gyuen agaynst chauceler length endyghted hunnys deth grete whyle pryson coclusyo neuer durst abyde tryal twelue men hys acquytayle fayn frendshyp gete beseche myndys sake shewe thought selfe therin pof trouth quod dyuerse suspycyouse thyngys layd agaynst hym al well substa cyally answered agayn hym yt vppon tellynge tale ofte tyme happeth wh sayde therin yet shall th thynke one way nother therfore though thynke iury whyche ryght honest men found verd cte theym selfe thought theyre owne conscyence trouthe yet myn owne mynde oughte eue herd therof lyfe helpe god could neuer thik yt pyf ben gyltye quod frende wolde neuer haue sued hys pyes quod ryght wyse men haue herd say ere thys wyll neuer refuse neyther goddys pardon kyngys wysdom mater many suspycyouse talys neuer false stade twelue mennys mouthes one may fynd surer way thynke veryly yf gyltye sholde neuer haue goten hys pardon al yt th neuer trowe brought thys worlde prynce benygne nature mercyfull mynde y souerayne lorde reygneth longe mo e reygne vppon v wherby neuer kynge coulde fynde hys hart frely forgyue forgete offe cys done comytted vnto hym self yet hath hys hyghnesse suche feruent affe cio right iustyce men causys teder zele conseruacio hys subgect whose lyuys hys hygh wysedom consydereth many stand parell geuyng perdon wylfull murderer neuer kyng byleue yt euer ware crown thys realme whych hath many yerys geue vnto fol e fewe therfore make selfe sure wylfull purpe sed cruell dede thys bene yf hyt bene trew frendys could haue bene founden chauncellour thys world could neuer haue goten hys pardon passe wyse yt vppon reporte cyrcumstancys kyng hygh prudence whych wyth flatery perceth depe bo ome dowtefull mater euer saw man lyfe well perceyued hys innocecye sythe e yly byleue yf bene gyltye neuer coud haue gotten hnous murder eny pardon hy y hyghnes dare make selfe mych bold innocency ye shall v derstad neuer sued pardon therfore b longe examynacyon mater well chauncellour othe beynge endyghted dede arrayned v pon entyghtement hy gi bench pled yltie thervppon kyn y grace beynge well suffycyently enformyd trouthe hys blyssed dysposycyon wyllig shold hys name eny false mater maynt ynyd g ue comaudemet hys n confesse theyr plees trewe wythout ny farther troble thing faythfull prynce clere declaracyon meter layd chauncellour urte selfe good fayth told byfore neuer hard lyfe yet haue herd wen yt well could sayed therin eny thing moued partyes herde thynke shold gyltye pand bysydys al thys consyde ing hunne well knowe hym saye dede though fayre dealer among hys neygbours yet man hygh mynded set glory vyctory whyche hoped haue premunyre wherof mych hosted sayed among hys famylyare frendys trusted spoke long dayes haue hys mater rys termys called hunnys case whych whan perceyued wolde go agaynst purpose temporall law shold wynne spurrys ouer spyrytuall law perceyued myche hys secrete sorys vnwrapped dyscouered bega fall fere worldly shame yt y mych lykely werynes hys lyfe rydde hym selfe therof whych maner affectyon se seldom happe specyally syth deuyll myght peraduenture ioyne therwt malycyouse hope yt whyche happed suspycyon hys deth myth layed charge parell chauncellour thys y say myche lykely thynge wherof neuer herd lyke byfore bysshoppys chaunceler shold kyll lollardys towre sore suspect covycte heresye wherby myght brynge hym selfe besynes yf hated man kyll hym wolde ye wote well yf loued hym myght easely brynge hym shame peradueture shamefull deth also pin good fayth q frend wyste yt trew heretyque dede parell proued wold well thynke malyce dyspayre hanged hym selfe pgod quod knoweth thynge trouth haue herd therin shall shew pmy selfe preset poulys wha bysshype ye presence ye mayre aldremen cytye codempned hym heretyque hys dethe redde e ly ye deposyons whych yt well proued conuyc e well dyuerse heresyes mysbyleue toward holy sacrement wter thervppon iudgement geuen hys body sholde burned yt pnow quod full profe assure bysshop wyse man vertuouse cunyng pby saynt mary quod profe better mych pi shall tell quod nother thyng wh che whan ye ye shall peraduenture byleue yt yet better pthat wolde gladly know quod farer neuer man hym sus ec e eny suche th e byfore pforsoth quod tel yt happ remember syx seue yere hune thus hanged hys body burned heretyke one essex carpenter vsed make pumpes whyche entended wyth suche hym selfe grete robbery thervppon brought vnto courte comaundement kyngys grace grete honourable estate thys realme selfe hym examynacyon wherin among thyngys confessed longe holden dyuers heresyes whych sayd hys brother beyng clerke chyrche taught bothe hys father hym promyse heresyes heygth shewed v connynge maysters scole herd rede specyally place whych named v londo sayd yt suche heretyques wont resorte theyr redyngys chamber mydnyght wh n asked hym ye namys wont haunte mydnyghte lecturis rehersed v dyuers amonge named rychard way wha asked hym man yt hune spake tolde v hys person hys howse sayd mary q went tourney whan cam thense agayne herd say hanged lollardys towre hys body burned heretyque thus lerned longe hune haunted heretyques lecture nyght long whych declared vnto kyngys hyghnesse confessed hys hyghnesse though sory yt eny man shold lewd yet hyghly dyd reioyce ye goodnes god broughte suche hyd myschyefe lyght kyngys comaundement manys brother examynacyo dyd dede confesse nothyng neyther ye felonyes heresyes yet brother dyd abyde anowed theym hys face wyth suche markys token yt myghte well appere sayd treuth surely meruayle yf wold fasly haue fayned heyghnouse thyng agaist hys owne brother hys owne father hym selfe beynge therto nothynge co pelled put eyther payne fere father dede could come myght ferther examyne nyght scole sauynge whych told co fessed thys mater shewed v also ye fyrst tyme one man london taken good honest whyche sayd scoler also hys brother heresyes whych man hys honestie forbare medle tyl shold haue tother brother sone handy comytted marshalsye thys man whych tolde de cted vnto v heretyque scoler hys came labour sue hym pretendynge dyd yt cheryte mych thought could fayle wha wold haue hym forbare therfore examyne hym tyll sholde haue examyned tother labored ware wyse shold dysapoynted hym myshapped yt dede yt hys beyng labor whose scoler heresie detecte hys howse sodaynly stryken slayne wreched ende consyence dyed wyth god knoweth tell ferther pby saynt iohn quod frend vppon ye hole tale yt semeth clere hunne hym selfe clere mater psurely quod semed yt far cowlde wytte vnto many euer herd yt wolde yet wene haue semed clerely yf present thexamynacyos sene vnder maner man came forthe therwith pbut yet quod frende englysh byble thoughe hunne hym selfe heretyque yet myght boke good ynough good reason y good boke shold burned wyth euyll man pye call well home quod put well mynd yt thyng wherby ye toke occasyon talke hunne talked longe last forgoten byleue well answered mynde fully satysfyed eny wyse good therwt onys ouerloked red aduysedly consydered boke pthe xvi chapyter pthe messenger reherseth som causys whych hath herd layd som clergye handy theyr mother tonge pi wente q proued playnly kepe yt haue shewed kepe none frome theym suche translacyon eyther yet approued good redy reproued naught wyclyffys tyndals olde onys wyclyffys day remayn lawful folkys handy red pye say well quod yet woman say somwhat yt alway ye cat wynked whan eye oute surely y yt nought ye englysh byble mennys handy whan many wold fayn haue yt pthat y trouth q thynke though fauourers secte heretyques feruent settynge theyr sect let lay theyr money togyder make purse amonge pryntyng euyll made euyll translated boke whych though yt happe forboden burned yet som solde ere spyed eche theym lese theyr parte yet thynk ther wyll prynter lyghtely hote put eny byble prent hys charge wherof losse sholde lye hole hys owne necke hange vppon doutfull tryall whyther fyrst copy hys translacyon made wyclyffys dayes synnys yf yt made synnys yt must approued byfore pryntynge surely howe yt hathe happed thys whyle god hathe eyther suffred prouyded eny good vertuouse man hath mynde faythfull wyse translate yt thervppo eyther clergye lest wyse somone bysshop approue yt thys thynge tell howe euer yt haue herd myche spoken mater mych dout made ther peraduenture yt wold let wythdrawe eny one bysshop admyttyng therof wythout assent remanaunt many thyngys layd agaynst yt yet y mynde one thyng putteth good men clergye dout suffer yt thys yt se somtyme myche worse sort feruent callyng yt fynde far better whych maketh theym fere lest men desyre yt good lest yf yt euery manys hand wold gret parell aryse sedycyouse people shold harme therwyth tha god honest folke sholde take frute therby whyche fere promyse thyng fereth euer wolde theyre malyce foly take harme thynge y yt self ordeyned men good wold neuer thauoydyng theyr harme take frome profyte whyche myght take thyng deserue lese ellys yf thabuse good thyng shold cause takynge awaye therof frome wolde vse yt well cryst shold hym selfe neuer haue ben borne brought hys fayth worlde god sholde neuer haue made yt neyther yf shold ye losse wold dapned wreches haue kepte away thoccasyon reward theym wold wyth helpe hys grace endeuoure theym deserue yt pi sure q frende ye dowt full hole youre mynd thys laues theyre tonge therwyth lewde theyre lyuynge money force lytell stele robbe murder myght many tymes wyth dysclosynge suche thyngys gete myche theym wolde kyll man le yet fynde neuer eny man take hym selfe lyne twayne dyscouereth wet abowte hyde boke bysyde ye shall vnderstand albeyt made boke hym self yet made wold yt shold seme haue ben mannys makynge hys thentent suche worshypfull wordys yt fayth dede man y man sayd though yt thyng wythout good work yet whan yt y ioyned wyth good workys meryt cometh fayth onely part therof workys god gyueth v heue fayth onely nothynge ou workys though gyue faythe yf lacke good workys yet yf haue regardeth hys rewarde workys eny thyng onely fayth sayde thys cause say fayth causeth saluacyon pto thys yt answered yf thys opynion true yet yt well appered thys y thynge mene wordys luther pomerane archeretyques secte playne saye yt yt y sacrylege go please god eny good workys fayth onely shold good work ioyned fayth shold god exacte good workys v wherof shold serue yf nothyng pl saunt god whan luther sayth nothyng dampne eny crysten man onely lacke byleue sheweth manyfestely onely nede good workys wyth fayth also haue faythe none euyll workys hurte v meaneth playnely fayth onely wt eny good workys ioyned therto also wyth kynd euyll workys ioyned therto y suffycyet saue v therfore yf ye hys secte yt sayde man ye auoyde thys y doctryne euer ye colour yt pthan yt ferther asked hym yf theyr meanyng shold sayd sholde moue hym felowes thynke fayth good workys ioyned together good workys nothinge worthe meryte shold fayth thanke reward shold gyuen fayth ryght ought good workys p answered many textys scrypture enduced theym ther vnto specyal textys saynt poule fides iustificat fayth iustyfyeth credidu abraam deo et reputatu est ad iusticiam abraam byleued god yt accompted hym iustyce si ex operibus habet quidem gloriam sed non apud deum yf iustyfyed workys tha glory wt god si ex operibus crist pro nobis gratis mortuus est iustyfyed work tha dyd cryst dye v naught grat redepti estis ye redemed frely therby maye se oure workys parte cause yet specyally wordys sauyour cryst sayd mych moued mynd wher sayth qui crediderit et baptisatus fuerit saluus erit byleueth y baptysed shall saued cryst requyryth nothyng fayth pby textys sayd playnly appered saluacyon cam faythe abraam iustyfyed fayth work yf good workys shold cause saluacyon saynt poule sayth cryst dyed nought neded dye v yf workys myght saue v redemed frely yf shold redeme selfe wyth payement oure owne workys pto yt answered textys alledged purpose sygnyfye none faythe cryst brought worlde incarnacyon passyo blessyd sauyour men le ged bounde obseruaunce moyses law law moyses good workys man able saue one man selfe wythout fayth cryst frely redemed v neyther euer shall haue eny reward v bytter paynes taken hys blyssed passyon v neuer deserued vnto hym sholde mych v fyrste faythe prechynge therof fyrst iustyfycacyon man therby sacrament fruyte baptysme gyuen world eny good workys euer world wrought goddys mere lybetal goodnes yet y neuer texte eny scrypture met baptysme fayth onely shall saue v wythout good workys yf lyue haue reason though sayd mouth sauyour byleueth shall saued nothyng speketh eny good work yet meaneth byleueth shall saued wythout good workys yf lyue theym ellys sholde ye well say men shall saued kepynge commaudementys wyth fayth syth cryst sayth yf wyl e entred kyngdome heue kepe commaundementys sayth also thou shalt haue lyfe whyche tyme spake worde eny fayth sayth also holy scrypture date clemosina et omnia muda sunt vobis gyue almoyse y clene whyche wordys yf men sholde largely conster pre mynence almoyse dede ye th luther secte constre textys speke fayth myght take false glose colour say faythe penaunce eyther eny vertue almoyse dede alone suffyseth saluacyon wredehedly euer lede lyfe bysyde yf sholde saye almoyse dede shold say wrong ye whan ye say fayth lyke wyse yt y vnderstand fayth must nedys go wt good workys yf shall frutfull though yt spoke te speke good workys yt vnderstanden theym whych baptysme haue tyme reason worke well good workys must walke wyth fayth sorow harte fawte good workys yf fayth shall aught auayle yf good work fynall repentaunce lacke good work fayle v hauyng tyme reason lyke fare myche worse fayth yt thys y thus maye well know textys holy scrypture yf set theym together take one text part set nother nought pto thys answered albe yt textys set togeth r proue fayth alone doth suffyse wythoute good workys whych thynge sayde hym selfe denyed yet sayd yt none textys proue eny thyng contrary whan fayth good workys ioyned together meryte cometh yet fayth onely nothyng workys p whervnto answered though dede text scrypture proued contrary yet syth y none sayth hole chyrch sayth byleueth co trary reason haue ye say gyue hole meryte vnto fayth parte rewarde good workys haue ye myche le reson whan playne wordys holy wryt openly contrary dyd god saye cain yf thou well thou shalte haue well sayth cryst theym dothe almoyse good measure shaken together heped runnynge ouer shall gyue bosome doth lorde shewe day iugement wyl gyue kyngdom heuen theym haue done almoyse mete drynke clothe lodgyng bycawse theyr charyte vsed dedys whyche dedys thoughe wyll rewarde wyth heuen excepte fayth went wt yet yf wrought fayth promyseth reward workys theyr fayth ferforth yt appereth wordys oure sauyoure placys hys wordys whyche sayd wold daye iudgement speke fayth wrought wonder hys name wythout good workys cheryte whome wolde tha bydde walke worker wyckednesse tell theym knoweth theym thyngys saye yt well appereth manys fayth neuer great yet yf good workys fayle hym hys fayth shall fayle heuen pthan sayd yet agayne fayth neuer wythoute go workys yf haue fayth fayth shal fayle ceace bryng forth fruyte good workys tre bryngeth forth hys leuys p yt answered hym page page labour payne thappostles toke prechynge naught synfull tormentys yt martyr suffered theyr passyon together synne ye dedys ch ryte cryst shall hym self sayth reward wyth euerlastynge lyfe g nerall dgement syn gether saynt poule rekened wyse sayd boldely hym self bonu certamen certaui cursu consumm et nuc superest michi corona iu itie haue laboured stryuen good stryfe haue perfourmed course lac eth crowne iustyce p therunto answered saynt powle wolde saye dedys suff cyent theym self oure suffycyency y god whervnto yt answered thys lytell mater y fayth suffycyent yt selfe suffycyency therof y also god hat lord wyth endeuo r gyueth v grace byleue yt ly eth lorde hys goodnes hyghly reward yt surely true saynt poule sayth th non sut condigne passiones h vite ad futuram gloriam que reuelabitur euer suffer thys worlde y worthy glory come shall shewed v thyng cowld sely wr ched creature suffer god brefe tyme thys short lyfe yt might ryght requyre rewarded euerlastyngly wyth suche ym ble ioy neyther ye hathe seen tonge expresse hart ymagyne conceyue yt also true th fayth ue ca haue hys n ture lytel myche lesse deserue heue good ded gret thig god grete thing coulde aske hym ryght bycause byleue hi though mych beholde vnto v yt vouchesaufe truste hym though hys worshyp hunge handy hys estymacyon lost yf credence wt v therfore amonge many folysh wordys luther folyshe euer heretyque spoke neuer sp e frantyque tha saythe yt god hath nede faythe saythe god hath nede good workys hath nede faythe hathe nede sholde byleue hym trouthe y yt nedeth neyther fayth oure workys syth hath determyned tha wyll saue v wythoute yf dyscrecyon haue therfore haue nede bothe yet neyther tone tot er together bytwene theyre owne nature worthy rewarde heuen se one ounce gold wherof x pownde weyghte hys owne nature toward worth one ouce whete one hundred pownde weyght therof nature selfe worthe one sely shepe y yet among men pryce appoynted agreed worth many hole shepe many pownde weyght brede hath yt lyked lyberall goodnes god set well fayth oure dedys whyche ellys twayn theyr owne nature ryght lytell value hygh pryce non y able bye theym paye hym self bycawse shold work th hym haue none pay mayster notte chapma sell ware worke vnto hym except wolde mad towardys hym vnkynd yt wold sell yt nother lesse nather hym leuer trauayle far sell lesse wold sell theyre neyghbours home folysh ypocryt rather tha wold sell theyr worke god euerlastynge ioy heuen sell yt world peuysh plesure ye vayn prayse puffed pore mortall mennys mouthes wyth blast wynde punto thys sayd true yt yt workys toke theyre value pryce thacceptacyo god lyst allowe sayd god reiected dysalowed set nought workys infydelys wrought wythout fayth sine fide impossibile est placere deo wtout fayth yt ipossyble please god faythfull chosen peple byleue trust hym accepteth alloweth dedys sayd wel proued wordys saynt iohn nichil danationis est hiis qui sunt christo iesu albe yt rehersyng comunycacyo wyth thys man yt may well yt reme braunce maye partely mysse order partely peraduenture adde ysh parte mater yet thys poynt assure faythfully y maner chaug varyauce opynyon many shyftys brought yt playnly thys poynt last felows luther secte fermely opynyon byleued god worketh euery good workys badde howe yt suche foreknoweth dapned maner workys profyfable god taketh theym nought neuer good tother syde hath chose fro ye begynnig predestynate glory work good ynog god accepteth taketh well worth neuer bad pit asked hym whyther yt forsakynge cryst peter alowed well approued cryste whyther yt aduour maslaugh ter god wel alowed dauyd pwherunto sayd bycause chose saye quod person god predestynate glory turne hym good euyll euer thys coclusyon declared theyr playn mynde opynyon clockys set vppon mater byfore make yt seme mened theyr word none harme yt clerely appered hys f whych theyr prechyng couertly craftely secte oute dampnable secte luther hoope ga e alway tyme whych truste opely boldely play raueno w luys deuoure shepe marre ye hole flok yt mene facys one hode neuer saw eny yt veryly play yt pagaute thys kynde suche prech prechyng peple make vysage though came strayght fro heuen teche new better way trew chyrche techeth hath taught many hudred yere ye chyrch examynacyon shew selfe pore mydle erth though taught none wyse tha ye chyrch doth co clusyo whe well examyned wt mych worke falsehode theyr cloked collusyo y pulled appereth ye malycyous trechery poyson put forthe vnder cloke hony thys yt tell laborynge yt myghte many meanes make yt seme prechig yt faith alon sufficiet saluacyo yt good work nothig worth nothig entended well accordyng ye doctryne ye chyrch yt hys felowes neuer ment otherwyse tha ye chyrch meneth yet coclusyo playnly shewed hym selfe yt hys felows entend therby brynge ye peple thys poynt last yt thyng handgeth onely vppon desteny lybertye manys wyll shold serue ryght nought menys ded good bad made dyfference afore god hys chosen people nothyng myslyketh hym yt neuer bad tother sort nothyng pleseth hym yt neuer good worst moste scheuouse heresye yt euer thoughte vppon therto moost madde yt y sayde vnto hym yf trew wherto preche counsayle eny man thynge fruyte cowlde come theyre exhortacyon yf shold hange vppon destenye shewed vnto hym many thyngys reprofe vnreasonable detestable heresye textys whyche alledged nothynge made hys purpose alledged saynt powle y dampnacyon theym cryste iesu sensuall appetytys shalbe dapned fayth cryst elli shold folow vpo false opinio god accept wel workys predestynate synne synne ye tother sort god hath predestynate y yt myche say may lawfully nought man lawfully thefte aduoutery lawfully manquellour lawfully forswere hym selfe goddys good sonny hys specyall chosen chyldren pnow alledged wordys saynt powle q iuste omnia cooperantur bonu iuste man holy martyr somtyme ye syn whych good man y goddys sufferaunce mytted fall y occasyon hym gretter good thauoydyng gretter syn theschewynge hyghe spyrytuall pryde whyche peraduenture contynuall c urse hys vertuous lyfe might deuyls subtyll suggestyon haue brought hym whereas one foule act lechery hath shewed hym f ayletye stede pryde broughte hym penaunce humylyte make hym runne faster forward vertue bycawse hath letted syt styll whyle syn therfore wyll runne forthe wynne agayne hys waye byfore caste hym selfe behynde yt ment euer theyr synnys turned good accepted rewarded better theyr euyll dedys god remytteth synnys chosen people forbereth impute blame therof vnto bycawse hys chosen people accepteth folk theyr person theyr merytys haue synned punyssheth wel theym somtyme bycause theym worketh ye tone sorte tother theyr dedes hym selfe alone nothyng therin theym selfe god whose goodnes iestymable doth dampne hounge nomber people intollerable intermynable torme tys hys pleasure vnderstanden farre agaynst naturall reason vtterly subuertyng vertue good order world hyghly blasphemig goodnes maieste almyghty god heuen yt wo der eny man erthely hath eyther one sparke wyt hys hed toward god man one droppe good wyll harte shold abhorre yt thys execrable heresye maketh god cause euyl cruell appetyte neuer tyrannte tormentour ascrybe benygne nature almyghty god auyour cryst toke vppo hym self syn hys endles pytye bare payne theym sake dampnable heresye holdeth god shold fyrst vntrew sholde laye vnto v wyght blame hys owne fawtys y wyt euyll workys whyche say wrought v v god dehortacyons comynacyons threttys scrypture god calleth men fro synne euyll workys yf world onys mynde byleued luther doth eny euyll dede hym selfe god doth theym hym selfe euery man y eyther chosen vnchosen yf chosen sorte none euyll dede dampne v yf vnchosen sorte good dede auayle v thus byleueth careth doth excepte fere temporall lawys worlde yet yf hys false faythe strong forceth lytell theym also shall thynke dyenge hys bed galows cometh deseruyng hangethall vppon destenye therfore lawys set nought hold man y bounden obay eny wold lybertye byleue lyst lyst say god doth v deserue hymselfe howrly theyr owne experyence theym selfe whan wyll thyng yt wh n lyst leue yt say theym selfe alone wythout god hys assystence y alway hand yf wyllyng worke therwyth lyght present ye sonne yf lyst wylfully set eyen wynke pwherof shold serue lawys bycome good order among men yf euery mysordered wretche myghte alledge hys myscheuous dede destyny pyf fre wyll serue nought euery mannys dede y hys desteny men complayn vpon eny except wyll say bycause yt y theyr desteny wyll angry wyth punysh heretyques except wyll saye bycawse yt y theyre desteny yf wyll hold theym theyre secte say men wrong burne theym theyre heresyes bycawse yt theyr desteny heretyques may well answered wyth theyr owne wordys one theyr sect serued good town almayne whyche robbed man brought byfore ye iudges coulde denye dedde sayd yt hys desteny yt therfore myghte blame hi answered hym hys doctryne yf yt hys destenye stele therfore muste holde hym excused yt also theyr desteny hange hym therfore must well holde theym excused agayne vndowtedly amonge men taker awaye fre wyll maye neuer auoyde answer reason fall wretch desperate wayes deuyls dampned sowlys tha fall raylyng reprouyng iustyce god say hym selfe wrought deuyls blame almyghty god sythe say lytell care dede hell heuen wold thys world lyue leud lybertye haue runne ryot syth se suffred theyre secte allowed iudgement deuyse wayes gete many fal theyr sorte mene god shall whyle worke theym many mery pastymes wherin yf theyre heresye onys page neuer bygon wyth vyolence thoughe vsed wayes coud allecte ye peple prechyng though therwt done luther dothe luther folowers whyche amonge theyr heresyes holde playn concl syon yt yt y lyefull eny crysten n fyght agaynst turke make agaist hym ny resystece though come crystendom wyth great de roy th say cryste men bounden cousayles cryst whyche say forboden defende self saynt peter ye rehersed reproued sauyour wha strake lchus ere albe yt dyd yt defence hys mayster moost innocent man euer vnto lay ye sayd begynnyng syth tyme crysten men fyrst fell fyghtynge yt hath ne r encreaced alwaye mynysshed decayed thys day turke hath estrayted v nere brought yt wythin ryghte narrow compare narrower shall sowing scysmes sedycyos among crysten people lay los e ther wythstandyng turkes inuasyon resystynge hys malyce sholde rather yf eny reason theyr heddys lay yt contrary whan cryste pryncys dyd theyr deuoyre agaist myscreast infydelys storyes monumentys ynoughe wytnes e manyfest ayde helpe god grete vyctoryes gyuen good crysten pryncis almyghty hand tother syde synnys thambicio crysten ruler desyryng eche others mynyon haue set theym dedly dyssenssyon amonge self wherby whyle eche hathe aspyred neynge hys haue ytell forced came comen corp crystendome god r gynge theyr inordynate appet hath wythdrawen hys helpe shewed careth lytell su ynge whyle eche laboreth turke prosper ferforth procede yf theyr blynde lo e therto shall fayle whyche oure lor forbede wythin shorte proce e swalowe p nd lbe yt cry forb de saynt peter beyng preste vnder hymself prynce hys prestys fyght wyth ye temporall sworde towarde thempechement resystence hys fruteful passyon wheruppo depeded ye saluacyo forth fay ly tha doth answere slenderly hys le mater poyntys playnely con utyd olde holy father yt yt sene myche byfore yt ben lykely haue shorted myche parte long comunicacion pfor trouth q wha consyder ye party well rede luther wu tyndals pla e wher layed ryshes woder yt either eny almayne could ly e e tone englyshe man ye tother pi myche meruayle quod ough many lyke well sych y eth pletye nought wonder y yf vycyouse folke fauoure theyr lyke whe theyr hartys onys fyxed vppon theyre blynde eccyons man may wyth myche frute prech poste reason wyth theym contrary thynge po der y resonably
